<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Autumn Term 2013</h2>
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday October 2nd</strong><br /><strong>Eleonora Bergman</strong>, Jewish Historical Institute, Warsaw<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/emanuel-ringelblum" target="_self">An Extraordinary Archive: Emanuel Ringelblum and the Warsaw Ghetto</a></strong><br />Lecture 7 pm, Lecture Theatre 2, Cruciform Building<br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday  October 3rd </strong><br />RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Kyle McCarter</strong>, Johns Hopkins University<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/law-cosmology-ancient-israel">Law and Cosmology in Ancient Israel </a></strong><br />Lecture 7pm,  Pearson  G22<br />Reception (drinks and light refreshments) 8pm, Garden Room, Wilkins building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday October 10th</strong><br /><strong>Chris Schilling</strong>, University of Buenos Aires<br /><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-identity-israeli-foreign-policy"><strong>Jewish Identity and Israeli Foreign Policy </strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Pearson  G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong> Thursday October 17th </strong><br /><strong>Francois Guesnet</strong>, Sidney and Elizabeth Corob Reader in Modern Jewish History Department of Hebrew and Jewish Studies, UCL<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/beilis-at-100-jewish-political-agency">Beilis at 100. A Reflection on Jewish Political Agency One Hundred Years After the Last Ritual Murder Trial in Europe</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong> Monday  October 21st </strong><br />LUCIAN GUBBAY LECTURE sponsored by the Sephardi community of London<br /><strong> Aron Rodrigue</strong>, Stanford University<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/sephardim-holocaust-diasporic-memory-jews-from-rhodes"> Sephardim, Holocaust, and Diasporic Memory: The Jews from the Island of Rhodes </a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Garden room, Wilkins building<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre </p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday October 30th </strong><br />LEONARD SAINER MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Timothy Snyder</strong>, Yale University<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/rescue-during-holocaust">Rescue during the Holocaust: Sources and Causes</a> </strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Pearson  G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />




<h6 class="heading"></h6>


<p class="p"><strong>Monday November 11th</strong><br />In conjunction with the ANGLO ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY<br /><strong>Kay Prag</strong>, Manchester Museum<br /><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/david-to-nehemiah"><strong>David to Nehemiah: new fragments from Kenyon's Jerusalem</strong></a><br /></p>
<p class="p"><strong>CHANGE OF VENUE: now 6.00 pm in Lecture Theatre G6 on the ground floor at the Institute of Archaeology, 31-34 Gordon Square</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday November 18th </strong><br /><strong>Keith Morgan</strong><br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/rutas-closet">Book Launch: Ruta's Closet</a></strong><br />Lecture 6.45pm,  Pearson G22<br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday November 21st</strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Theo Dunkelgrün</strong>, University of Cambridge<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/hebrew-manuscript-medieval-england">The Amazing Adventures of a Hebrew Manuscript from Medieval England</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday  November  27th </strong><br /><strong>Philippe Sands</strong>, UCL<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/my-father-the-good-nazi">My Father the Good Nazi: Reflections on an
Encounter</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick G08<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday  December 4th</strong><br /><strong>Jeremy Hicks</strong>, Queen Mary University of London<br /><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/first-films-of-the-holocaust">First Films of the Holocaust:  Soviet Cinema and the Genocide of the Jews, 1938-1946</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Pearson  G22<br /></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Autumn 2014 Public Lectures</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday October 22nd </strong><br />BOOK LAUNCH<br /><strong>Philipp Nothaft,</strong> UCL<br /><strong>Medieval
Latin Christian Texts on the Jewish Calendar</strong><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Gustave Tuck lobby <br />
Lecture 6.45 pm, Gustave Tuck lecture theatre, 2<sup>nd</sup>
floor, Wilkins Building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday October 29th </strong><br />RAYMOND WESTBROOK
MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Peretz Segal</strong><strong>, </strong>Israeli
Ministry of Justice<strong><em> </em></strong><br /><strong>The Binding of Isaac and the Expulsion of Ishmael
as a  </strong><strong>Model for the Faith of Abraham</strong><br />Lecture 7.00 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building     <br />Reception 7.45pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday November 5th </strong><br />In conjunction with
the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Richard Cohen</strong><strong>, </strong>Hebrew University, Jerusalem<br /><strong>The Visual Moses Mendelssohn (1769-2014): the
Philosopher </strong><strong>as an Icon</strong><br />Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden
Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 13th </strong><br /><strong>Dominic Lieven</strong><strong>, </strong>University of Cambridge<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/empires-nationalisms-first-world-war">Empires, Nationalisms and the First World War</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45 pm<strong><br /></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 20th</strong><br /><strong>Jan Grabowski</strong>, University of Ottowa<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/hunt-for-the-jews-occupied-poland">Hunt for the Jews: The case of Occupied Poland, 1942-1945</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building    <br />Lecture 6.45 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 27th</strong><br /><strong>Vanessa Freedman, </strong>UCL<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/moses-gaster-and-his-world"><strong>The Man who never threw anything away: Moses
Gaster </strong><strong>and his World</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Chadwick G08, Chadwick Building<br />Lecture 6.45 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday December 1st</strong><br />In conjunction with
the ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY<br /><strong>Ilaria Bultrighini, </strong>UCL<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-christian-tombstones-ancient-zoara">Christian and Jewish Tombstones from ancient
Zoara/Zoora</a></strong><br />Lecture 6.00 pm, followed by reception<br />Institute of Archaeology Lecture theatre, Gordon Square</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday December 11th</strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Jonathan Romain</strong>, Maidenhead Synagogue</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/royal-jews"><strong>Royal
Jews – Jewish Life in Berkshire from the Readmission </strong><strong>Till Today</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Please  check our webpage TO CONFIRM LECTURE DETAILS
IF YOU PLAN ON ATTENDING AS THE PROGRAMME MAY BE SUBJECT TO LAST-MINUTE CHANGES.</strong></p>
<p class="p">You can also email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520     </p>
<p class="p"><strong><sup> </sup></strong></p>
<p class="p">All
events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<p class="p">Prior booking is recommended
through Eventbrite </p>
<p class="p">Free admission,
voluntary contributions welcome<br /></p>
<p class="p"><strong>THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</strong></p>
<p class="p">  Charity Registration
No.213114</p>

  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }
  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);

})();

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">PUBLIC LECTURE SERIES AUTUMN 2015</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> Wednesday October 7th </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Michael Berkowitz, Francois Guesnet, </strong>UCL</p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/european-jewish-migration"><strong>The European Jewish Experience of Migration: Early Modern and Modern Perspectives</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">6.30 pm, Garden Room, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson
Building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday October 12th</strong></p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY<strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mark Merrony, </strong>University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/Archaeologists-collectors-museums"><strong>Archaeologists, Collectors, and Museums: Redressing the Ethical Divide in the face of Modern Conflict</strong></a></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday October 15th</strong> </p>
<p class="p"> JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND PRESIDENTIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Philip Alexander, </strong>Manchester University</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-community-dublin"><strong>&quot;In the footsteps of King Billy&quot;: The Origins of the Jewish Community in Dublin in the Context of Irish History</strong></a></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15 pm, Chadwick G08<br /></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday October 29th</strong> </p>
<p class="p">  RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Tessa Rajak, </strong>University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/rediscovery-of-josephus-and-modern-jewish-identity">The Rediscovery of Josephus and Modern Jewish Identity</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm, followed by reception, <strong>JZ Young lecture theatre, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <em> </em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday November 4th</strong></p>
<p class="p">BOOK LAUNCH<strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Helen Jacobus, </strong>UCL</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/zodiac-calendars-and-angels-in-the-dead-sea-scrolls"><strong>Zodiac Calendars and Angels in the Dead Sea Scrolls </strong></a></p>
<p class="p">  Reception from 6.30 pm, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson Building</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Tuesday November 10th</strong></p>
<p class="p">  LEON YUDKIN MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Jonathan Magonet, </strong>Leo Baeck College / Seinan Gakuin University, Fukuoka</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/moses-jewish-problem"><strong>Moses’ Jewish Problem</strong></a></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm, followed by reception, <strong>JZ Young lecture theatre, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 19th </strong> </p>
<p class="p">  In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Elliott Horowitz</strong>, University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/biblical-ishmael-as-seen-by-medieval-and-modern-jews">The Biblical Ishmael as seen by Medieval and Modern Jews</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15 pm, Chadwick G08</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br />Monday November 30th</strong> </p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/piano-concert">PIANO RECITAL</a><strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mignonette Aarons, </strong> London</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Includes works by Jewish composers at Terezín</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Recital 7pm, Haldane Room, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p"> PLEASE NOTE THERE WILL BE A COLLECTION FOR THE PIANIST AT THIS EVENT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Please  check our webpage TO CONFIRM LECTURE 
DETAILS IF YOU PLAN ON ATTENDING AS THE PROGRAMME MAY BE SUBJECT TO 
LAST-MINUTE CHANGES.</strong></p>
<p class="p"> You can also email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520   </p>
<p class="p"> <strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> All events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<p class="p"> Prior booking is recommended through Eventbrite</p>
<p class="p"> Free admission, voluntary contributions welcome<br /></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Charity Registration No.213114</p>

  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }
  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (win.attachEvent) {
    win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);

  doc.close();
})();

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Public Lectures Autumn 2016</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday October 20th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/Wandering-Jews-in-Englands-Green-and-Pleasant-Land">Wandering Jews in England’s Green and Pleasant
Land</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Daniel Langton, </strong>The
University of Manchester</p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /></p>
<p class="p">Reception 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room. </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7pm, J.Z. Young lecture theatre. </p>
<p class="p"> UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street WC1E 6BT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday November 9th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/persuasion-or-coercion-approaches-to-the-law-early-jewish-and-christian-thought"><strong>Persuasion or Coercion? Approaches to the law in </strong><strong>early Jewish and Christian thought</strong></a><strong><em></em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>David Satran, </strong>Hebrew University of Jerusalem</p>
<p class="p">RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00pm, Roberts 106 followed by
reception in the Roberts Building foyer   <strong></strong></p>
<p class="p">UCL, Torrington Pace, WC1E 7JE</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday November 17th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/a-new-approach-mapping-jewish-history">A New Approach to Mapping Jewish History</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Nicholas de Lange, </strong>University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p">Reception 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room. Lecture 7pm, J.Z. Young lecture theatre. </p>
<p class="p">UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street WC1E 6BT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday November 30th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/digitalising-hebrew-manuscripts">Digitalizing Hebrew Manuscripts</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Ilana Tahan, </strong>The
British Library </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00pm, UCL <strong>Garwood lecture theatre</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday December 5th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/synagogue-of-dura-europos-and-its-place-in-local-society"><strong>“An Even More
Unexpected Find” – </strong><strong>the Synagogue of </strong><strong>Dura-Europos and its Place in Local Society</strong></a><em><strong> </strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Ted Kaizer, </strong>Durham University</p>
<p class="p">In conjunction with the Anglo-Israel Archaeological Society</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 6.00pm, Harrie Massey
Lecture Theatre (E8), 25 Gordon Street, London WCIH OAY </p>
<p class="p">Followed by refreshments, Leventis
Gallery, Institute of Archaeology, 31-34 Gordon Square,
WC1H 0PY</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday
December 15th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/naphtali-franks-musician-synagogue-warden-and-communal-eminence"><strong>Naphtali Franks FRS (1715-1796) – Musician,
Synagogue </strong><strong>Warden and Communal Eminence</strong></a><strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Stephen Massil, </strong>Jewish
Historical Society of England</p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p">Reception 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room. Lecture 7pm, J.Z. Young lecture theatre. </p>
<p class="p">UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street WC1E 6BT </p>

(function(){
  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }
  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (win.attachEvent) {
    win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);
  }

  iframe.src = "javascript:void(0)";
  iframe.title = ""; iframe.role = "presentation";
  (iframe.frameElement || iframe).style.cssText = "width:0;height:0;border:0;display:none;";
  where = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
  where.parentNode.insertBefore(iframe, where);

  try {
    doc = iframe.contentWindow.document;
  } catch(e) {
    dom = document.domain;
    iframe.src="javascript:var d=document.open();d.domain='"+dom+"';void(0);";
    doc = iframe.contentWindow.document;
  }
  doc.open()._l = function() {
    var js = this.createElement("script");
    if (dom) { this.domain = dom; }
    js.id = "boomr-if-as";
    js.src = "//c.go-mpulse.net/boomerang/" +
    "SUWW2-HAKPB-Q4WN7-TQ6VL-GTMT2";
    BOOMR_lstart=new Date().getTime();
    this.body.appendChild(js);
  };
  doc.write('<body onload="document._l();">');
  doc.close();
})();
</script>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Autumn Lectures 2012</h2>
<p class="lead"> Thursday November 8th</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#vered" target="_self"><em>Vered Shemtom, Stanford University</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Dwelling in the Text: The Concept of Bayit in Contemporary Hebrew Literature</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">  Wednesday November 14th</p>
<p class="lead"> With the Anglo-Israel Archaeological Society</p>
<p class="p"> <em><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#thorn" target="_self">Amara Thornton, UCL</a></em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Exploring, Training, Conserving: The Role of the British School of Archaeology in Jerusalem in Mandate Palestine</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">   Wednesday November 21st</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#hakak" target="_self"><em>Yohai Hakak, University of Portsmouth</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mental Health Specialists and Inter-Faith Relationships: the Unholy Union between Religion and Therapy in Contemporary Israel</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">  Monday November 26th</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#pschl" target="_self"><em>Lisa Peschel, University of York</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Jewish Theatre during the Holocaust: Recently Rediscovered Scripts from the Theresienstadt Ghetto</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="p">  Thursday December 6th
</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#zha" target="_self"><em>Zohar Hadromi-Allouche, University of Aberdeen</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>The Second Fall of Adam and Eve: Biblical Aspects of an Islamic Narrative</strong></p>
<p class="p">  Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">  Thursday December 13th</p>
<p class="lead"> Abrahams-Curiel Memorial Lecture</p>
<p class="p"> <em>Robert Segal, University of Aberdeen</em><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#ras"></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>King Saul as Mythic Hero</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="p"> <em>All events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Just turn up - Free Admission - voluntary contributions welcome</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p">
THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</p>

	<h2 class="heading">Autumn Term 2011</h2>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>December 12th</strong> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p">Nathan Abrams, Bangor University</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The New Jew in Film- Exploring Jewishness and  Judaism in Contemporary Cinema</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#n_abrams" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>December 8th</strong> JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND PRESIDENTIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Ada Rapoport-Albert, UCL </p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Women in HaBaD Hasidism</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><em></em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#ada_r_a" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>December 1st</strong> ARNOLD LEE MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Charlotte Fonrobert, Stanford University</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Ritualising the Neighbourhood: the Eruv as </strong><em><strong>Jewish Topography</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#fonrobert" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>November 24th</strong> BOOK LAUNCH WITH THE LEO BAECK INSTITUTE</p>
<p class="p">Cathy Gelbin, University of Manchester</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Golem Returns: From German Romantic  Literature to Global Jewish Culture, 1808-2008 </strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#c_s_gelbin" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>November 14th </strong>WITH THE ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHEOLOGICAL SOCIETY</p>
<p class="p">David Jacobson, UCL, Nikos Kokkinos, UCL, Tessa Rajak,  University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Herod the Great as Ruler and Builder –  a panel discussion in memory of Ehud Netzer 1934-2010</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#d_jacobson" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>October 31st</strong>  ABRAHAMS-CURIEL MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Paolo Aranha, Warburg Institute, London</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Goa Inquisition and the Repression of the ‘New Christians’ of Jewish origin in the 16th-18th Centuries</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#p_aranha" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>October 27th</strong> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p">Solomon Abramovich, Imperial College London</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Smuggled in Potato Sacks - Stories of the Hidden Children of the Kaunas Ghetto</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#s_abramovitch" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>September 22nd</strong> WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY  ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p">Geoffrey Cantor,University of Leeds/UCL</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Anglo-Jewry in 1851: The Great Exhibition and Political Emancipation</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#g_cantor" target="_self">More...</a></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Tenth Jakobovitz Lecture in Jewish Medical Ethics</h2>
<p class="p"><strong>11th May 2010<br /></strong></p>
<p class="p">Rabbi Professor Michael J Broyde</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Can a Physician Assist in Coercive Interrogation?<br />A Jewish View of Military Ethics<br />with a Focus on the Role of the Doctor</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Michael J. Broyde</strong> is professor of law at Emory Law and the academic director of the Law and Religion Programme at Emory University. His primary areas of interest are law and religion, Jewish law and ethics, and comparative religious law. Besides Jewish law and family law, Professor Broyde has taught Federal Courts, Alternative Dispute Resolution, Secured Credit and Bankruptcy.</p>
<p class="p">Professor Broyde is ordained as a rabbi by Yeshiva University and is a member of the Beth Din of America, the largest Jewish law court in America. He was the director of that court during the 1997-1998 academic year. Professor Broyde is also the founding rabbi of the Young Israel synagogue in Atlanta and a founder of the Atlanta Torah MiTzion kollel study programme.<br /><br />Professor Broyde has published more than 75 articles and book chapters on various aspects of law and religion and Jewish law, including &quot;A Jewish Law View of World Law,&quot; (Emory Law Journal 2005), about how Jewish law might classify international law, and a series of vigorous exchanges in several publications on military ethics in Jewish law. He also has published a number of articles in the area of federal courts, including an article in the &quot;Harvard Journal of Law and Public Policy&quot; on the impeachment process. He is the Editor of the Journal of Halacha and Contemporary Society.<br /><br />Professor Broyde has authored, edited and co-edited several volumes including Human Rights in Judaism (1997), Marriage, Divorce and the Abandoned Wife in Jewish Law: A Conceptual Understanding of the Agunah Problems in America (2001) and Marriage, Sex and Family in Judaism (2005). His first book, The Pursuit of Justice and Jewish Law (1996) has recently been revised and re-published (2007).<br /><br />T<em>his meeting has been arranged jointly between the Jewish Medical Association (UK)<br />and the Institute of Jewish Studies at University College London</em><br /></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">SPRING/SUMMER 2015 PUBLIC LECTURES</h2>
<p class="p"><strong> Wednesday February 4th </strong></p>
<p class="p">SIMON WIESENTHAL MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Dan
Michman, </strong>Bar-Ilan University</p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/goal-of-the-nazi-anti-jewish-enterprise">What exactly was the goal
of the Nazi anti-Jewish enterprise?</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday February 11th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Bezalel Porten, </strong>Hebrew University, Jerusalem</p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/elephantine-to-jerusalem-and-back">From Elephantine to Jerusalem and Back</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday February 19th</strong> </p>
<p class="p">In
conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Derek Penslar, </strong>University of Toronto</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Between Honour and Authenticity: Zionism as
Theodor Herzl’s Life Project</strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday
March 30th</strong> </p>
<p class="p"> All-day symposium with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"><strong>In
honour of David Ruderman, </strong>scholar-in-residence, JHSE</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Mission and Missionaries among the Jews in
19th Century Europe</strong></p>
<p class="p">Gustave Tuck Lecture theatre, second Floor, Wilkins Building  (full programme details to
be announced)</p>
<p class="p"><em> </em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday May 11th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Yuval Sinai, </strong>Yale University </p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/maimonides-and-contemporary-tort-theory">Maimonides and Contemporary
Tort Theory: Law, Religion, Economics and Morality </a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30 pm, Haldane
Room, Wilkins Building </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday May 21st</strong></p>
<p class="p"> In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL
SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Lucia
Raspe, </strong>Johann Wolfgang Goethe
University, Frankfurt</p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jews-saints-medieval-rabbi"><strong>Do Jews Believe in
Saints? A Medieval Rabbi and his Posthumous Travels</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">Reception
from 6.30 pm, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson
Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture  7.00 pm </p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday May 28th </strong> </p>
<p class="p"> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Lily Kahn</strong>, UCL </p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/grammar-eastern-european-hasidic-hebrew-tale">The Grammar of the Eastern European Hasidic
Hebrew Tale</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Haldane Room, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Tuesday June 2nd</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Launching</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/history-of-jewish-warsaw"><strong>Ephemeral Metropolis? The History of Jewish Warsaw</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">6.00 - 8.00 pm, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson Building (North East entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday June 10th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Evelyn M. Cohen</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-women-books-medieval-renaissance-italy">Jewish Women and Books in Medieval and Renaissance Italy</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Gustave Tuck lecture theatre, 2nd floor, Wilkins Building </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm </p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday
June 25th</strong></p>
<p class="p">In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Anthony
Grafton, </strong> Princeton University</p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/early-modern-views-of-the-last-supper"><strong>How Jesus celebrated Passover: Early Modern Views of the Last Supper </strong></a></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Public Lectures Spring 2016</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday January  21st</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/popes-jews-16-century-italy">The Popes and the Jews in 16th Italy: a convoluted encounter</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Piet van Boxel</strong><br /></p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /></p>
<p class="p">Evening lecture</p>
<p class="p">Drinks served from 6.30pm followed by Lecture at 7.00pm   <br />Venue: G46 (HO Schild Pharmacology lecture theatre), Medical Sciences building, UCL<br />Entrance via Malet Place, off Torrington Place</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday February 4th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jews-in-finland-during-world-war-two">Brothers-in-arms with Nazi Germans: Jews in Finland during World War II</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Simo Muir</strong></p>
<p class="p">Lecture
at 5.30pm</p>
<p class="p">Venue: Chadwick G08, Chadwick Building, UCL, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday March 2nd</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/future-of-the-past-jewish-history-shadow-and-hope">The future of the past: Reflecting on Jewish history under the signs of shadow and hope</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Rainer Kampling</strong></p>
<p class="p">Simon Wiesenthal Memorial Lecture at 6.30pm</p>
<p class="p">Venue: J.Z. Young
lecture theatre, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of the main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday March
9th</strong></p>
<p class="p">The 'Jewish Indian Theory’: The Problem of the Origin of the American Populations</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Nathan Wachtel</strong></p>
<p class="p">Venue: Gustave Tuck lecture theatre. Followed by a reception in the South Cloisters</p>
<p class="p">Lecture in
conjunction with UCL Institute of the Americas at <strong>5.30pm</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday March
17th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://jhse.org/event/the-first-sephardim-in-the-atlantic/">The first Sephardim in the Atlantic</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>David Abulafia</strong></p>
<p class="p">Richard Barnett Memorial Lecture in
conjunction with the Jewish Historical Society of England time t.b.a.</p>
<p class="p">Venue: Gavin de Beer
room, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT </p>
<p class="p">(just south of the main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Tuesday July 26th – Wednesday July 27th</strong></p>
<p class="p">The IJS summer conference</p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-languages-conference">Jewish Languages</a></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Spring 2014 Public Lectures</h2>


<h4 class="heading">64th Public Lecture Series - Spring 2014</h4>




<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Tuesday January 21st </strong><br />BOOK LAUNCH<br /><strong>Joanna Michlic, </strong>Bristol University<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/memory-holocaust-postcommunist-europe"><strong>Bringing the Dark to Light - Memory of the Holocaust in <br />Postcommunist Europe </strong></a><br />Lecture 6pm, Institute of Archaeology lecture theatre, 31-34 Gordon Square<br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday January 30th </strong><br />BOOK LAUNCH<br /><strong>Toby Greene, </strong>BICOM<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/blair-labour-palestine">Blair, Labour and Palestine: Conflicting Views on Middle East Peace After 9/11</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday February 13th </strong><br />ABRAHAMS-CURIEL MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Donald Sassoon, </strong>Queen Mary University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jews-making-modern-cultural-industry">Jews and the Making of the Modern Cultural Industry</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Terrace Restaurant, Wilkins building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Garwood lecture theatre, South Wing (first floor)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday February 27th </strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Todd Endelman, </strong>University of Michigan<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/redcliffe-salaman-president-jewish-historical-society-england">Redcliffe Salaman, President of the Jewish Historical Society of England</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building <strong><br /></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> Wednesday March 5th</strong><br />
IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE SIMON WIESENTHAL CENTRE IN THE UNITED KINGDOM<br /><strong>Robert Wistrich</strong>, Hebrew University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/ambivalence-betrayal-left-jews-israel">From Ambivalence to Betrayal: The Left, the Jews and Israel</a></strong><br />
Reception from 6.00pm in the Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building </p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday March 13th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Katarzyna Person</strong>, Jewish Historical Institute, Warsaw<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/postwar-quest-for-justice"><strong>The Postwar Quest for Justice: Jewish Honor Courts in Poland</strong> <strong>and in the Displaced Persons' Camps</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday March 20th</strong><br /><strong>Itzik Gottesman, </strong>Yiddish Forward<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/about-jewish-folklore" target="_self"><strong>What's Jewish About Jewish Folklore?</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Haldane Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <br /><strong>Wednesday March 26th</strong><br /><strong>Devorah
Wainer, </strong>The University of Sydney</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/judaism-human-rights"><strong>Can Judaism restore the ‘Human’ to Human Rights?</strong></a><br />Lecture 7.15pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday March 27th</strong><br /><strong>Yosef Kaplan, </strong>Hebrew University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/christobal-mendez-abraham-franco-silveyra-converso">Christobal Mendez alias David Mendez: The Puzzling Saga of a 17th Century Converso</a></strong><br />Reception from 6pm, Terrace Restaurant, Wilkins building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday April 24th</strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Nadia Valman</strong>, Queen Mary University<br /></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-women-writers-victorian-england"><strong>Jewish Women Writers in Victorian England</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p">   MORE EVENTS MAY BE ADDED!<br />PLEASE CHECK OUR WEBPAGE FOR CHANGES AND UPDATES<br /></p>
<p class="p"> <br />You can also join the free mailing list for regular information<br />email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk" target="_self">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520.</p>
<p class="p"> <br />All
 events take place at University College London. Booking through 
Eventbrite is advised, see our website or mailshots for each event.<br />Admission is free but voluntary contributions are welcomed<br />THE IJS IS A CHARITY SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!<br />Charity Registration No.213114 <br /></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Spring Term 2011</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="lead">May 12th Screening</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Undzere kinder (Our Children)</strong>,  a Yiddish film (with English subtitles) made in 1948The film is one of the only postwar movies made in Yiddish and almost the last full length yiddish film to be made.  It was also the first film which attempted to deal with the Holocaust.  Suppressed by the postwar Polish Communist goernment as &quot;pro -Zionist&quot; and lost for over 30 years, <em>&quot;Our Children</em>&quot; was largely shot on location at an orphanage/school near Lodz.  It stars children who were actual survivors of the Holocaust and focuses on how they came to terms with their past.</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Discussion between Shimon Redlich, Sir Martin Gilbert, and Antony Polonsky on Jewish life in postwar Poland</strong></p>
<p class="p"><em>This event was made possible with the cooperation of UCL-SSEES </em></p>
<p class="p"><em>The Department of Hebrew and Jewish Studies</em></p>
<p class="p"><em>The Institute of Polish-Jewish Studies, Oxford</em></p>
<p class="p"><em>Polish Cultural Institute, London</em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>March 8th</strong> ELLIOTT PHILIPP MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Eva-Maria Ziege, CJCR, Cambridge<em>n</em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em><em><strong>The Fra</strong></em><em><strong>kfurt School and antisemitism</strong></em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="lead">March 1st</p>
<p class="p">Judith Schlanger, Paris </p>
<p class="p"><strong>Between the Beit-din and the Royal Exchequer:Hebrew documents from medieval England</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 24th</strong> RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Yoram Cohen, Tel Aviv University</p>
<p class="p"><strong><em>Politics, Diplomacy, Gift exchange and Royal Marriages in the Late Bronze Age (1500-1200BCE)</em></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="lead">February 11th</p>
<p class="p">Timothy Snyder, Yale University</p>
<p class="lead"><em>Bloodlands: Europe Between Hitler and Stalin</em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 9th</strong></p>
<p class="p">Dvora Bregman, Ben-Gurion University </p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Escape from Vasto: Complaints of a 15th century Italian Rabbi</strong></em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 1st</strong></p>
<p class="p"><em>Avraham Gross, Ben-Gurion University </em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em><em><strong>Liturgy as a Collective and Personal Memorial of 1096</strong></em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><em><strong></strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong>January 24th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><em>Shamma Friedman, Jewish Theological Seminary of America </em></p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Now You See it, Now You Don’t: Can Source- Criticism Perform Magic on Talmudic Passages about Sorcery?</strong></em></p>

	<h2 class="heading">Spring Term 2012</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday, 30th May</strong></p>
<p class="p">David Sorkin</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Beyond the Secular-Religious Dichotomy: Four
Characteristics of the Religious Enlightenment</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/beyond_dichotomy" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday, 21st May</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Henny Brenner and Michael Brenner<br /></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>From Experience, to Memoir, to History: Henny Brenner in Nazi Dresden</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/from_experience" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>April 23rd</strong></p>
<p class="p">Yohanan Petrovsky-Shtern</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Crime and Punishment in the Shtetl (1790-1850)</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/crime_and_punishment">More...</a><br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>April</strong><strong> 8th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> Amy-Jill Levine<br /> </p>
<p class="p"><strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><em>Violence
on the Jerusalem-Jericho Road:</em></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><em> Readings and Misreadings of the Parable
of the Good Samaritan</em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/bios_2012/#levine" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday, 4th April</strong></p>
<p class="p">Daniel Greene<br /></p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Jewish Origins of an American Idea: The Menorah Association and Cultural Pluralism</strong></em><a href="/silva/ijs/All_Events/jewish_origins"><br /></a></p>
<p class="p"><a href="http://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/jewish_origins" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>March </strong><strong>22nd</strong></p>
<p class="p">Stephan Feuchtwang, LSE  <br /></p>
<p class="p"><strong><em>Loss and Repair: a Berlin Jewish mixed heritage family</em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/bios_2012/#feuchtwang" target="_self"><strong>More...</strong></a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>March</strong> <strong>5th</strong><em> </em><em> BOOK LAUNCH </em></p>
<p class="p"> ABRAHAMS-CURIEL MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Elizabeth Schächter<em>, </em>University of Kent</p>
<p class="p"> <strong><em>The Jews of Italy, 1848-1915: Between Tradition and Transformation</em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/bios_2012/#schachter" target="_self">More...
</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> February </strong><strong>27th</strong><br /></p>
<p class="p"> Sharman Kadish, Jewish Heritage UK <br /></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><em>The Synagogues of Britain and Ireland: An Architectural and Social History</em></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/bios_2012/#kadish" target="_self">More...
</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 22nd</strong> <em>BOOK LAUNCH </em></p>
<p class="p"> David Conway, UCL <em><br /></em></p>
<p class="p"> <em><strong>Jewry in Music</strong> <br /></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/bios_2012/#conway" target="_self">More...</a> <br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 14th</strong> LEONARD SAINER MEMORIAL LECTURE 
</p>
<p class="p">Shmuel Feiner,  <em>Bar Ilan University</em> <br /></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Summer Term 2011</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><em><br /></em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><em>June 1st  2011 </em></strong>BOOK LAUNCH AND LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"><br />Ada Rapoport-Albert<br /><br /><em><strong>Women and the Messianic Heresy of Sabbatai Zevi, 1666-1816</strong></em><br /><br /><br />Women are conspicuously absent from the Jewish mystical tradition.  Only the<br />chance survival of scant evidence suggests that, at various times and places, individual Jewish women did pursue the path of mystical piety or prophetic spirituality, but it appears that they were generally highly censured. This contrasts sharply with the fully acknowledged prominence of women in the mystical traditions of both Christianity and Islam.<br /><br />It is against this background that the mystical messianic movement centred on the personality of Sabbatai Zevi (1626-76) stands out as a unique and remarkable exception. Sabbatai Zevi addressed to women a highly original liberationist message, proclaiming that he had come to make them 'as happy as men' by releasing them from the pangs of childbirth and the subjugation to their husbands that were ordained for women as a consequence of the primordial sin. This unprecedented redemptive vision became an integral part of Sabbatian philosophy, which the messianists believed to be unfolding.<br /><br />Their New Law, superseding the Old with the dawning of the messianic era, overturned the traditional Jewish norms that distinguished and regulated relations between the sexes. This was expressed not only in the outlandish ritual transgression of sexual prohibitions, in which Sabbatian women were notoriously implicated, but also in the apparent adoption of the idea  -alien to rabbinic Judaism- that virginity, celibacy, or sexual abstinence were conducive to women's spiritual empowerment.<br /><br />Ada Rapoport-Albert's latest book traces the diverse manifestations of this vision in every phase of Sabbatianism and its offshoots. </p>
<hr class="rule" />

<h3 class="heading"><em>Undzere kinder (Our Children)</em></h3>





<p class="p"><em></em><br /><strong>June 13th  2011</strong><br /><br /><em><strong>Undzere kinder</strong> is a Yiddish film (with English sub-titles) made in 1948<br />The film is one of the only postwar movies made in Yiddish and almost the last full-length Yiddish film to be made. It was also the first film which attempted to deal with the Holocaust. Suppressed by the post-war Polish Communist government as 'pro-Zionist' and lost for over 30 years, Our Children was largely shot on location at an orphanage/school near Lodz. It stars children who were actual survivors of the Holocaust and focuses on how they come to terms with their past.<br /></em><br /></p>


<!-- end main slot where silva content gets rendered-->

(function(){
  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }
  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (win.attachEvent) {
    win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);
  }

  iframe.src = "javascript:void(0)";
  iframe.title = ""; iframe.role = "presentation";
  (iframe.frameElement || iframe).style.cssText = "width:0;height:0;border:0;display:none;";
  where = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
  where.parentNode.insertBefore(iframe, where);

  try {
    doc = iframe.contentWindow.document;
  } catch(e) {
    dom = document.domain;
    iframe.src="javascript:var d=document.open();d.domain='"+dom+"';void(0);";
    doc = iframe.contentWindow.document;
  }
  doc.open()._l = function() {
    var js = this.createElement("script");

    this.body.appendChild(js);
  };
  doc.write('<body onload="document._l();">');
  doc.close();
})();

<p class="p">The
IJS Autumn programme will be available shortly. Watch this space, and if you
are not on our mailing list please email <a href="mailto:s.benisaac@ucl.ac.uk">s.benisaac@ucl.ac.uk</a>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Autumn Term 2013</h2>
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday October 2nd</strong><br /><strong>Eleonora Bergman</strong>, Jewish Historical Institute, Warsaw<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/emanuel-ringelblum" target="_self">An Extraordinary Archive: Emanuel Ringelblum and the Warsaw Ghetto</a></strong><br />Lecture 7 pm, Lecture Theatre 2, Cruciform Building<br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday  October 3rd </strong><br />RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Kyle McCarter</strong>, Johns Hopkins University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/law-cosmology-ancient-israel">Law and Cosmology in Ancient Israel </a></strong><br />Lecture 7pm,  Pearson  G22<br />Reception (drinks and light refreshments) 8pm, Garden Room, Wilkins building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday October 10th</strong><br /><strong>Chris Schilling</strong>, University of Buenos Aires<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-identity-israeli-foreign-policy"><strong>Jewish Identity and Israeli Foreign Policy </strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Pearson  G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong> Thursday October 17th </strong><br /><strong>Francois Guesnet</strong>, Sidney and Elizabeth Corob Reader in Modern Jewish History Department of Hebrew and Jewish Studies, UCL<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/beilis-at-100-jewish-political-agency">Beilis at 100. A Reflection on Jewish Political Agency One Hundred Years After the Last Ritual Murder Trial in Europe</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong> Monday  October 21st </strong><br />LUCIAN GUBBAY LECTURE sponsored by the Sephardi community of London<br /><strong> Aron Rodrigue</strong>, Stanford University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/sephardim-holocaust-diasporic-memory-jews-from-rhodes"> Sephardim, Holocaust, and Diasporic Memory: The Jews from the Island of Rhodes </a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Garden room, Wilkins building<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre </p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday October 30th </strong><br />LEONARD SAINER MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Timothy Snyder</strong>, Yale University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/rescue-during-holocaust">Rescue during the Holocaust: Sources and Causes</a> </strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Pearson  G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />




<h6 class="heading"></h6>


<p class="p"><strong>Monday November 11th</strong><br />In conjunction with the ANGLO ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY<br /><strong>Kay Prag</strong>, Manchester Museum<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/david-to-nehemiah"><strong>David to Nehemiah: new fragments from Kenyon's Jerusalem</strong></a><br /></p>
<p class="p"><strong>CHANGE OF VENUE: now 6.00 pm in Lecture Theatre G6 on the ground floor at the Institute of Archaeology, 31-34 Gordon Square</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday November 18th </strong><br /><strong>Keith Morgan</strong><br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/rutas-closet">Book Launch: Ruta's Closet</a></strong><br />Lecture 6.45pm,  Pearson G22<br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday November 21st</strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Theo Dunkelgrün</strong>, University of Cambridge<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/hebrew-manuscript-medieval-england">The Amazing Adventures of a Hebrew Manuscript from Medieval England</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday  November  27th </strong><br /><strong>Philippe Sands</strong>, UCL<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/my-father-the-good-nazi">My Father the Good Nazi: Reflections on an
Encounter</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick G08<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday  December 4th</strong><br /><strong>Jeremy Hicks</strong>, Queen Mary University of London<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/first-films-of-the-holocaust">First Films of the Holocaust:  Soviet Cinema and the Genocide of the Jews, 1938-1946</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture  6.45pm, Pearson  G22<br /></p>

(function(){
  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }
  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (win.attachEvent) {
    win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);
  }

  iframe.src = "javascript:void(0)";
  iframe.title = ""; iframe.role = "presentation";
  (iframe.frameElement || iframe).style.cssText = "width:0;height:0;border:0;display:none;";
  where = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
  where.parentNode.insertBefore(iframe, where);

  try {
    doc = iframe.contentWindow.document;
  } catch(e) {
    dom = document.domain;
    iframe.src="javascript:var d=document.open();d.domain='"+dom+"';void(0);";

  };
  doc.write('<body onload="document._l();">');
  doc.close();
})();

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Autumn 2014 Public Lectures</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday October 22nd </strong><br />BOOK LAUNCH<br /><strong>Philipp Nothaft,</strong> UCL<br /><strong>Medieval
Latin Christian Texts on the Jewish Calendar</strong><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Gustave Tuck lobby <br />
Lecture 6.45 pm, Gustave Tuck lecture theatre, 2<sup>nd</sup>
floor, Wilkins Building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday October 29th </strong><br />RAYMOND WESTBROOK
MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Peretz Segal</strong><strong>, </strong>Israeli
Ministry of Justice<strong><em> </em></strong><br /><strong>The Binding of Isaac and the Expulsion of Ishmael
as a  </strong><strong>Model for the Faith of Abraham</strong><br />Lecture 7.00 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building     <br />Reception 7.45pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday November 5th </strong><br />In conjunction with
the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Richard Cohen</strong><strong>, </strong>Hebrew University, Jerusalem<br /><strong>The Visual Moses Mendelssohn (1769-2014): the
Philosopher </strong><strong>as an Icon</strong><br />Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden
Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 13th </strong><br /><strong>Dominic Lieven</strong><strong>, </strong>University of Cambridge<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/empires-nationalisms-first-world-war">Empires, Nationalisms and the First World War</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45 pm<strong><br /></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 20th</strong><br /><strong>Jan Grabowski</strong>, University of Ottowa<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/hunt-for-the-jews-occupied-poland">Hunt for the Jews: The case of Occupied Poland, 1942-1945</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building    <br />Lecture 6.45 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 27th</strong><br /><strong>Vanessa Freedman, </strong>UCL<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/moses-gaster-and-his-world"><strong>The Man who never threw anything away: Moses
Gaster </strong><strong>and his World</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15 pm, Chadwick G08, Chadwick Building<br />Lecture 6.45 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday December 1st</strong><br />In conjunction with
the ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY<br /><strong>Ilaria Bultrighini, </strong>UCL<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-christian-tombstones-ancient-zoara">Christian and Jewish Tombstones from ancient
Zoara/Zoora</a></strong><br />Lecture 6.00 pm, followed by reception<br />Institute of Archaeology Lecture theatre, Gordon Square</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday December 11th</strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Jonathan Romain</strong>, Maidenhead Synagogue</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/royal-jews"><strong>Royal
Jews – Jewish Life in Berkshire from the Readmission </strong><strong>Till Today</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, ground floor, Wilkins Building </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Please  check our webpage TO CONFIRM LECTURE DETAILS
IF YOU PLAN ON ATTENDING AS THE PROGRAMME MAY BE SUBJECT TO LAST-MINUTE CHANGES.</strong></p>
<p class="p">You can also email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520     </p>
<p class="p"><strong><sup> </sup></strong></p>
<p class="p">All
events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<p class="p">Prior booking is recommended
through Eventbrite </p>
<p class="p">Free admission,
voluntary contributions welcome<br /></p>
<p class="p"><strong>THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</strong></p>
<p class="p">  Charity Registration
No.213114</p>

  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);

})();

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">PUBLIC LECTURE SERIES AUTUMN 2015</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> Wednesday October 7th </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Michael Berkowitz, Francois Guesnet, </strong>UCL</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/european-jewish-migration"><strong>The European Jewish Experience of Migration: Early Modern and Modern Perspectives</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">6.30 pm, Garden Room, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson
Building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday October 12th</strong></p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY<strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mark Merrony, </strong>University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/Archaeologists-collectors-museums"><strong>Archaeologists, Collectors, and Museums: Redressing the Ethical Divide in the face of Modern Conflict</strong></a></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday October 15th</strong> </p>
<p class="p"> JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND PRESIDENTIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Philip Alexander, </strong>Manchester University</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-community-dublin"><strong>&quot;In the footsteps of King Billy&quot;: The Origins of the Jewish Community in Dublin in the Context of Irish History</strong></a></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15 pm, Chadwick G08<br /></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday October 29th</strong> </p>
<p class="p">  RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Tessa Rajak, </strong>University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/rediscovery-of-josephus-and-modern-jewish-identity">The Rediscovery of Josephus and Modern Jewish Identity</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm, followed by reception, <strong>JZ Young lecture theatre, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <em> </em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday November 4th</strong></p>
<p class="p">BOOK LAUNCH<strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Helen Jacobus, </strong>UCL</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/zodiac-calendars-and-angels-in-the-dead-sea-scrolls"><strong>Zodiac Calendars and Angels in the Dead Sea Scrolls </strong></a></p>
<p class="p">  Reception from 6.30 pm, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson Building</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Tuesday November 10th</strong></p>
<p class="p">  LEON YUDKIN MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Jonathan Magonet, </strong>Leo Baeck College / Seinan Gakuin University, Fukuoka</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/moses-jewish-problem"><strong>Moses’ Jewish Problem</strong></a></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm, followed by reception, <strong>JZ Young lecture theatre, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday November 19th </strong> </p>
<p class="p">  In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Elliott Horowitz</strong>, University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/biblical-ishmael-as-seen-by-medieval-and-modern-jews">The Biblical Ishmael as seen by Medieval and Modern Jews</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15 pm, Chadwick G08</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br />Monday November 30th</strong> </p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/piano-concert">PIANO RECITAL</a><strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mignonette Aarons, </strong> London</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Includes works by Jewish composers at Terezín</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Recital 7pm, Haldane Room, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p"> PLEASE NOTE THERE WILL BE A COLLECTION FOR THE PIANIST AT THIS EVENT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Please  check our webpage TO CONFIRM LECTURE 
DETAILS IF YOU PLAN ON ATTENDING AS THE PROGRAMME MAY BE SUBJECT TO 
LAST-MINUTE CHANGES.</strong></p>
<p class="p"> You can also email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520   </p>
<p class="p"> <strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> All events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<p class="p"> Prior booking is recommended through Eventbrite</p>
<p class="p"> Free admission, voluntary contributions welcome<br /></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Charity Registration No.213114</p>

	<h2 class="heading">Public Lectures Autumn 2016</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday October 20th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/Wandering-Jews-in-Englands-Green-and-Pleasant-Land">Wandering Jews in England’s Green and Pleasant
Land</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Daniel Langton, </strong>The
University of Manchester</p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /></p>
<p class="p">Reception 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room. </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7pm, J.Z. Young lecture theatre. </p>
<p class="p"> UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street WC1E 6BT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday November 9th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/persuasion-or-coercion-approaches-to-the-law-early-jewish-and-christian-thought"><strong>Persuasion or Coercion? Approaches to the law in </strong><strong>early Jewish and Christian thought</strong></a><strong><em></em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>David Satran, </strong>Hebrew University of Jerusalem</p>
<p class="p">RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00pm, Roberts 106 followed by
reception in the Roberts Building foyer   <strong></strong></p>
<p class="p">UCL, Torrington Pace, WC1E 7JE</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday November 17th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/a-new-approach-mapping-jewish-history">A New Approach to Mapping Jewish History</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Nicholas de Lange, </strong>University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p">Reception 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room. Lecture 7pm, J.Z. Young lecture theatre. </p>
<p class="p">UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street WC1E 6BT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday November 30th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/digitalising-hebrew-manuscripts">Digitalizing Hebrew Manuscripts</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Ilana Tahan, </strong>The
British Library </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00pm, UCL <strong>Garwood lecture theatre</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday December 5th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/synagogue-of-dura-europos-and-its-place-in-local-society"><strong>“An Even More
Unexpected Find” – </strong><strong>the Synagogue of </strong><strong>Dura-Europos and its Place in Local Society</strong></a><em><strong> </strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Ted Kaizer, </strong>Durham University</p>
<p class="p">In conjunction with the Anglo-Israel Archaeological Society</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 6.00pm, Harrie Massey
Lecture Theatre (E8), 25 Gordon Street, London WCIH OAY </p>
<p class="p">Followed by refreshments, Leventis
Gallery, Institute of Archaeology, 31-34 Gordon Square,
WC1H 0PY</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday
December 15th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/naphtali-franks-musician-synagogue-warden-and-communal-eminence"><strong>Naphtali Franks FRS (1715-1796) – Musician,
Synagogue </strong><strong>Warden and Communal Eminence</strong></a><strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Stephen Massil, </strong>Jewish
Historical Society of England</p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p">Reception 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room. Lecture 7pm, J.Z. Young lecture theatre. </p>
<p class="p">UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street WC1E 6BT </p>

(function(){
  if (window.BOOMR && window.BOOMR.version) { return; }
  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (win.attachEvent) {
    win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);

  iframe.title = ""; iframe.role = "presentation";
  (iframe.frameElement || iframe).style.cssText = "width:0;height:0;border:0;display:none;";

})();

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Autumn Lectures 2012</h2>
<p class="lead"> Thursday November 8th</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#vered" target="_self"><em>Vered Shemtom, Stanford University</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Dwelling in the Text: The Concept of Bayit in Contemporary Hebrew Literature</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">  Wednesday November 14th</p>
<p class="lead"> With the Anglo-Israel Archaeological Society</p>
<p class="p"> <em><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#thorn" target="_self">Amara Thornton, UCL</a></em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Exploring, Training, Conserving: The Role of the British School of Archaeology in Jerusalem in Mandate Palestine</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">   Wednesday November 21st</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#hakak" target="_self"><em>Yohai Hakak, University of Portsmouth</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mental Health Specialists and Inter-Faith Relationships: the Unholy Union between Religion and Therapy in Contemporary Israel</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">  Monday November 26th</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#pschl" target="_self"><em>Lisa Peschel, University of York</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Jewish Theatre during the Holocaust: Recently Rediscovered Scripts from the Theresienstadt Ghetto</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="p">  Thursday December 6th
</p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#zha" target="_self"><em>Zohar Hadromi-Allouche, University of Aberdeen</em></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>The Second Fall of Adam and Eve: Biblical Aspects of an Islamic Narrative</strong></p>
<p class="p">  Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="lead">  Thursday December 13th</p>
<p class="lead"> Abrahams-Curiel Memorial Lecture</p>
<p class="p"> <em>Robert Segal, University of Aberdeen</em><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2012/index/#ras"></a></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>King Saul as Mythic Hero</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.15pm, Chadwick meeting room. Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick Lecture Theatre</p>
<p class="p"> <em>All events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Just turn up - Free Admission - voluntary contributions welcome</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p">
THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</p>

  var dom,doc,where,iframe = document.createElement("iframe"),win = window;

  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    win.BOOMR_onload=(e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (win.addEventListener) {
    win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (win.attachEvent) {
    win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);
  }

  iframe.src = "javascript:void(0)";
  iframe.title = ""; iframe.role = "presentation";
  (iframe.frameElement || iframe).style.cssText = "width:0;height:0;border:0;display:none;";

  where.parentNode.insertBefore(iframe, where);

})();
