	<h2 class="heading">Autumn Term 2011</h2>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>December 12th</strong> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p">Nathan Abrams, Bangor University</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The New Jew in Film- Exploring Jewishness and  Judaism in Contemporary Cinema</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#n_abrams" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>December 8th</strong> JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND PRESIDENTIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Ada Rapoport-Albert, UCL </p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Women in HaBaD Hasidism</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><em></em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#ada_r_a" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong><strong><strong><em><strong><strong><em><strong><strong></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></em></strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>December 1st</strong> ARNOLD LEE MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Charlotte Fonrobert, Stanford University</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Ritualising the Neighbourhood: the Eruv as </strong><em><strong>Jewish Topography</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#fonrobert" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>November 24th</strong> BOOK LAUNCH WITH THE LEO BAECK INSTITUTE</p>
<p class="p">Cathy Gelbin, University of Manchester</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Golem Returns: From German Romantic  Literature to Global Jewish Culture, 1808-2008 </strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#c_s_gelbin" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>November 14th </strong>WITH THE ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHEOLOGICAL SOCIETY</p>
<p class="p">David Jacobson, UCL, Nikos Kokkinos, UCL, Tessa Rajak,  University of Oxford</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Herod the Great as Ruler and Builder –  a panel discussion in memory of Ehud Netzer 1934-2010</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#d_jacobson" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>October 31st</strong>  ABRAHAMS-CURIEL MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Paolo Aranha, Warburg Institute, London</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Goa Inquisition and the Repression of the ‘New Christians’ of Jewish origin in the 16th-18th Centuries</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#p_aranha" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>October 27th</strong> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p">Solomon Abramovich, Imperial College London</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Smuggled in Potato Sacks - Stories of the Hidden Children of the Kaunas Ghetto</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#s_abramovitch" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>September 22nd</strong> WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY  ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p">Geoffrey Cantor,University of Leeds/UCL</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Anglo-Jewry in 1851: The Great Exhibition and Political Emancipation</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/autumn_2011/speakers_autumn_2011/#g_cantor" target="_self">More...</a></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Tenth Jakobovitz Lecture in Jewish Medical Ethics</h2>
<p class="p"><strong>11th May 2010<br /></strong></p>
<p class="p">Rabbi Professor Michael J Broyde</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Can a Physician Assist in Coercive Interrogation?<br />A Jewish View of Military Ethics<br />with a Focus on the Role of the Doctor</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Michael J. Broyde</strong> is professor of law at Emory Law and the academic director of the Law and Religion Programme at Emory University. His primary areas of interest are law and religion, Jewish law and ethics, and comparative religious law. Besides Jewish law and family law, Professor Broyde has taught Federal Courts, Alternative Dispute Resolution, Secured Credit and Bankruptcy.</p>
<p class="p">Professor Broyde is ordained as a rabbi by Yeshiva University and is a member of the Beth Din of America, the largest Jewish law court in America. He was the director of that court during the 1997-1998 academic year. Professor Broyde is also the founding rabbi of the Young Israel synagogue in Atlanta and a founder of the Atlanta Torah MiTzion kollel study programme.<br /><br />Professor Broyde has published more than 75 articles and book chapters on various aspects of law and religion and Jewish law, including &quot;A Jewish Law View of World Law,&quot; (Emory Law Journal 2005), about how Jewish law might classify international law, and a series of vigorous exchanges in several publications on military ethics in Jewish law. He also has published a number of articles in the area of federal courts, including an article in the &quot;Harvard Journal of Law and Public Policy&quot; on the impeachment process. He is the Editor of the Journal of Halacha and Contemporary Society.<br /><br />Professor Broyde has authored, edited and co-edited several volumes including Human Rights in Judaism (1997), Marriage, Divorce and the Abandoned Wife in Jewish Law: A Conceptual Understanding of the Agunah Problems in America (2001) and Marriage, Sex and Family in Judaism (2005). His first book, The Pursuit of Justice and Jewish Law (1996) has recently been revised and re-published (2007).<br /><br />T<em>his meeting has been arranged jointly between the Jewish Medical Association (UK)<br />and the Institute of Jewish Studies at University College London</em><br /></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">SPRING/SUMMER 2015 PUBLIC LECTURES</h2>
<p class="p"><strong> Wednesday February 4th </strong></p>
<p class="p">SIMON WIESENTHAL MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Dan
Michman, </strong>Bar-Ilan University</p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/goal-of-the-nazi-anti-jewish-enterprise">What exactly was the goal
of the Nazi anti-Jewish enterprise?</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday February 11th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Bezalel Porten, </strong>Hebrew University, Jerusalem</p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/elephantine-to-jerusalem-and-back">From Elephantine to Jerusalem and Back</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday February 19th</strong> </p>
<p class="p">In
conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Derek Penslar, </strong>University of Toronto</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Between Honour and Authenticity: Zionism as
Theodor Herzl’s Life Project</strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday
March 30th</strong> </p>
<p class="p"> All-day symposium with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"><strong>In
honour of David Ruderman, </strong>scholar-in-residence, JHSE</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Mission and Missionaries among the Jews in
19th Century Europe</strong></p>
<p class="p">Gustave Tuck Lecture theatre, second Floor, Wilkins Building  (full programme details to
be announced)</p>
<p class="p"><em> </em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday May 11th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Yuval Sinai, </strong>Yale University </p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/maimonides-and-contemporary-tort-theory">Maimonides and Contemporary
Tort Theory: Law, Religion, Economics and Morality </a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30 pm, Haldane
Room, Wilkins Building </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday May 21st</strong></p>
<p class="p"> In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL
SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Lucia
Raspe, </strong>Johann Wolfgang Goethe
University, Frankfurt</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jews-saints-medieval-rabbi"><strong>Do Jews Believe in
Saints? A Medieval Rabbi and his Posthumous Travels</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">Reception
from 6.30 pm, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson
Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture  7.00 pm </p>
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday May 28th </strong> </p>
<p class="p"> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Lily Kahn</strong>, UCL </p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/grammar-eastern-european-hasidic-hebrew-tale">The Grammar of the Eastern European Hasidic
Hebrew Tale</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Haldane Room, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Tuesday June 2nd</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Launching</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/history-of-jewish-warsaw"><strong>Ephemeral Metropolis? The History of Jewish Warsaw</strong></a></p>
<p class="p">6.00 - 8.00 pm, Pearson Lecture theatre, Pearson Building (North East entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday June 10th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Evelyn M. Cohen</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-women-books-medieval-renaissance-italy">Jewish Women and Books in Medieval and Renaissance Italy</a></strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Gustave Tuck lecture theatre, 2nd floor, Wilkins Building </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm </p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday
June 25th</strong></p>
<p class="p">In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Anthony
Grafton, </strong> Princeton University</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/early-modern-views-of-the-last-supper"><strong>How Jesus celebrated Passover: Early Modern Views of the Last Supper </strong></a></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30 pm, Garden Room, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00 pm</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Please  check our webpage TO CONFIRM LECTURE DETAILS IF YOU PLAN ON ATTENDING AS THE PROGRAMME MAY BE SUBJECT TO LAST-MINUTE CHANGES.</strong></p>
<p class="p">You can also email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520   </p>
<p class="p"><strong><sup></sup></strong></p>
<p class="p">All events take place at University College London, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<p class="p">Prior booking is recommended through Eventbrite</p>
<p class="p">Free admission, voluntary contributions welcome<br /></p>
<p class="p"><strong>THE IJS IS SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!</strong></p>
<p class="p">Charity Registration No.213114</p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Public Lectures Spring 2016</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday January  21st</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/popes-jews-16-century-italy">The Popes and the Jews in 16th Italy: a convoluted encounter</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Piet van Boxel</strong><br /></p>
<p class="p">IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /></p>
<p class="p">Evening lecture</p>
<p class="p">Drinks served from 6.30pm followed by Lecture at 7.00pm   <br />Venue: G46 (HO Schild Pharmacology lecture theatre), Medical Sciences building, UCL<br />Entrance via Malet Place, off Torrington Place</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday February 4th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jews-in-finland-during-world-war-two">Brothers-in-arms with Nazi Germans: Jews in Finland during World War II</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Simo Muir</strong></p>
<p class="p">Lecture
at 5.30pm</p>
<p class="p">Venue: Chadwick G08, Chadwick Building, UCL, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday March 2nd</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/future-of-the-past-jewish-history-shadow-and-hope">The future of the past: Reflecting on Jewish history under the signs of shadow and hope</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Rainer Kampling</strong></p>
<p class="p">Simon Wiesenthal Memorial Lecture at 6.30pm</p>
<p class="p">Venue: J.Z. Young
lecture theatre, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of the main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Wednesday March
9th</strong></p>
<p class="p">The 'Jewish Indian Theory’: The Problem of the Origin of the American Populations</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Nathan Wachtel</strong></p>
<p class="p">Venue: Gustave Tuck lecture theatre. Followed by a reception in the South Cloisters</p>
<p class="p">Lecture in
conjunction with UCL Institute of the Americas at <strong>5.30pm</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday March
17th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://jhse.org/event/the-first-sephardim-in-the-atlantic/">The first Sephardim in the Atlantic</a></p>
<p class="p"><strong>David Abulafia</strong></p>
<p class="p">Richard Barnett Memorial Lecture in
conjunction with the Jewish Historical Society of England time t.b.a.</p>
<p class="p">Venue: Gavin de Beer
room, UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT </p>
<p class="p">(just south of the main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Tuesday July 26th – Wednesday July 27th</strong></p>
<p class="p">The IJS summer conference</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-languages-conference">Jewish Languages</a></p>

	<h2 class="heading">Public Lectures Spring 2017</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday January 12th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> IN CONJUNCTION WITH
THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Colin
Shindler</strong>, SOAS<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/anti-semitism-anti-zionism-and-the-left-in-britain">Anti-Semitism, anti-Zionism and the Left in Britain</a></strong><strong> </strong><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30pm, foyer,
UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of UCL main
entrance)</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm Gavin de
Beer lecture theatre</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday February 8th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> BOOK LAUNCH</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Carlotta
Ferrara degli Uberti,</strong> UCL<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Making Italian Jews – Family, Gender,
Religion and the Nation, 1816-1918</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30pm,
foyer UCL Engineering Building, Malet Place entrance, Torrington Place, London
WC1E 6BT </p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm Lecture
theatre 1:02</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday February 15th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Bezalel
Porten</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/the-book-of-jonah-a-paraphonous-polemic">The Book of Jonah: A Paraphonous
Polemic</a></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30pm,
foyer UCL Anatomy Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of UCL
main entrance)</p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm Gavin de
Beer lecture theatre</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Monday February 20th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Steven Fassberg,</strong> Hebrew University of Jerusalem<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Trends and Methodologies in the Study of Qumran Hebrew</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room </p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 7.00pm JZ Young
lecture theatre</p>
<p class="p"> UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of UCL main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday February 23rd</strong><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> IN CONJUNCTION WITH
THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Geoffrey Cantor, </strong>University of Leeds<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://jhse.org/event/jewish-chronicle-punch/"><strong>The Jewish Chronicle and Punch</strong></a><em></em></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room Lecture 7.00pm JZ Young lecture theatre</p>
<p class="p"> UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of UCL main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <em> </em></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday March 16th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> IN CONJUNCTION WITH
THE JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Tony Kushner, </strong>University of Southampton<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://jhse.org/event/jacob-harris-early-jewish-triple-murderer-england/"><strong>Jacob
Harris: an early Jewish murderer in England</strong></a><strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Reception from 6.30pm,
Gavin de Beer room Lecture 7.00pm JZ Young lecture theatre</p>
<p class="p"> UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of 
UCLmain entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday March 22</strong><sup>nd</sup></p>
<p class="p"> IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE ANGLO-ISRAEL ARCHAEOLOGICAL SOCIETY</p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Mark Geller</strong><strong>, </strong>UCL</p>
<p class="p"> <strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/is-there-such-a-thing-as-medicine-in-the-bible">Is there such a thing
as medicine in the Bible?</a></strong><strong><em></em></strong></p>
<p class="p"> Lecture 6.00pm J.Z.
Young lecture theatre followed by a reception in the foyer</p>
<p class="p"> UCL Anatomy Building,
Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of UCL main entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday March 23rd</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Jonathan Israel</strong><strong>, </strong>Princeton<strong></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Enlightenment and Jewish Emancipation: the Story of a failed Project</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong>Reception from 6.30pm, Gavin de Beer room </p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00pm Darwin lecture theatre</p>
<p class="p">UCL Anatomy Building/ Darwin Building, Gower Street, London WC1E 6BT (just south of  UCLmain entrance)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><br /></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Monday March 27th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong>Daniel Bodi</strong>, Sorbonne University<br /><strong>Abishag, the Administrator of King David’s Wives </strong></p>
<p class="p">Reception from 6.30pm, foyer UCL Roberts Building, Malet Place entrance</p>
<p class="p">Lecture 7.00pm Ambrose Fleming lecture theatre
</p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Spring 2014 Public Lectures</h2>


<h4 class="heading">64th Public Lecture Series - Spring 2014</h4>




<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Tuesday January 21st </strong><br />BOOK LAUNCH<br /><strong>Joanna Michlic, </strong>Bristol University<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/memory-holocaust-postcommunist-europe"><strong>Bringing the Dark to Light - Memory of the Holocaust in <br />Postcommunist Europe </strong></a><br />Lecture 6pm, Institute of Archaeology lecture theatre, 31-34 Gordon Square<br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday January 30th </strong><br />BOOK LAUNCH<br /><strong>Toby Greene, </strong>BICOM<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/blair-labour-palestine">Blair, Labour and Palestine: Conflicting Views on Middle East Peace After 9/11</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday February 13th </strong><br />ABRAHAMS-CURIEL MEMORIAL LECTURE<br /><strong>Donald Sassoon, </strong>Queen Mary University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jews-making-modern-cultural-industry">Jews and the Making of the Modern Cultural Industry</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Terrace Restaurant, Wilkins building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Garwood lecture theatre, South Wing (first floor)</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday February 27th </strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Todd Endelman, </strong>University of Michigan<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/redcliffe-salaman-president-jewish-historical-society-england">Redcliffe Salaman, President of the Jewish Historical Society of England</a></strong><br />Reception from 6.00pm, South Cloisters, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building <strong><br /></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong> Wednesday March 5th</strong><br />
IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE SIMON WIESENTHAL CENTRE IN THE UNITED KINGDOM<br /><strong>Robert Wistrich</strong>, Hebrew University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/ambivalence-betrayal-left-jews-israel">From Ambivalence to Betrayal: The Left, the Jews and Israel</a></strong><br />
Reception from 6.00pm in the Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building </p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday March 13th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>Katarzyna Person</strong>, Jewish Historical Institute, Warsaw<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/postwar-quest-for-justice"><strong>The Postwar Quest for Justice: Jewish Honor Courts in Poland</strong> <strong>and in the Displaced Persons' Camps</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Garden Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday March 20th</strong><br /><strong>Itzik Gottesman, </strong>Yiddish Forward<br /><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/about-jewish-folklore" target="_self"><strong>What's Jewish About Jewish Folklore?</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.15pm, Haldane Room, Wilkins Building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <br /><strong>Wednesday March 26th</strong><br /><strong>Devorah
Wainer, </strong>The University of Sydney</p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/judaism-human-rights"><strong>Can Judaism restore the ‘Human’ to Human Rights?</strong></a><br />Lecture 7.15pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Thursday March 27th</strong><br /><strong>Yosef Kaplan, </strong>Hebrew University<br /><strong><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/christobal-mendez-abraham-franco-silveyra-converso">Christobal Mendez alias David Mendez: The Puzzling Saga of a 17th Century Converso</a></strong><br />Reception from 6pm, Terrace Restaurant, Wilkins building<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Chadwick lecture theatre, Chadwick building</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Thursday April 24th</strong><br />In conjunction with the JEWISH HISTORICAL SOCIETY OF ENGLAND<br /><strong>Nadia Valman</strong>, Queen Mary University<br /></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/ijs-events-publication/jewish-women-writers-victorian-england"><strong>Jewish Women Writers in Victorian England</strong></a><br />Reception from 6.00pm, Pearson G23<br />Lecture 6.45pm, Pearson G22, Pearson Building NE entrance</p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p">   MORE EVENTS MAY BE ADDED!<br />PLEASE CHECK OUR WEBPAGE FOR CHANGES AND UPDATES<br /></p>
<p class="p"> <br />You can also join the free mailing list for regular information<br />email us on <a href="mailto:ijs@ucl.ac.uk" target="_self">ijs@ucl.ac.uk</a> or phone 020 7679 3520.</p>
<p class="p"> <br />All
 events take place at University College London. Booking through 
Eventbrite is advised, see our website or mailshots for each event.<br />Admission is free but voluntary contributions are welcomed<br />THE IJS IS A CHARITY SUPPORTED BY PEOPLE LIKE YOU!<br />Charity Registration No.213114 <br /></p>

	<h2 class="heading">Spring Term 2011</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="lead">May 12th Screening</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Undzere kinder (Our Children)</strong>,  a Yiddish film (with English subtitles) made in 1948The film is one of the only postwar movies made in Yiddish and almost the last full length yiddish film to be made.  It was also the first film which attempted to deal with the Holocaust.  Suppressed by the postwar Polish Communist goernment as &quot;pro -Zionist&quot; and lost for over 30 years, <em>&quot;Our Children</em>&quot; was largely shot on location at an orphanage/school near Lodz.  It stars children who were actual survivors of the Holocaust and focuses on how they came to terms with their past.</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Discussion between Shimon Redlich, Sir Martin Gilbert, and Antony Polonsky on Jewish life in postwar Poland</strong></p>
<p class="p"><em>This event was made possible with the cooperation of UCL-SSEES </em></p>
<p class="p"><em>The Department of Hebrew and Jewish Studies</em></p>
<p class="p"><em>The Institute of Polish-Jewish Studies, Oxford</em></p>
<p class="p"><em>Polish Cultural Institute, London</em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>March 8th</strong> ELLIOTT PHILIPP MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Eva-Maria Ziege, CJCR, Cambridge<em>n</em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em><em><strong>The Fra</strong></em><em><strong>kfurt School and antisemitism</strong></em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong></strong></p>
<p class="lead">March 1st</p>
<p class="p">Judith Schlanger, Paris </p>
<p class="p"><strong>Between the Beit-din and the Royal Exchequer:Hebrew documents from medieval England</strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 24th</strong> RAYMOND WESTBROOK MEMORIAL LECTURE</p>
<p class="p">Yoram Cohen, Tel Aviv University</p>
<p class="p"><strong><em>Politics, Diplomacy, Gift exchange and Royal Marriages in the Late Bronze Age (1500-1200BCE)</em></strong></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="lead">February 11th</p>
<p class="p">Timothy Snyder, Yale University</p>
<p class="lead"><em>Bloodlands: Europe Between Hitler and Stalin</em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 9th</strong></p>
<p class="p">Dvora Bregman, Ben-Gurion University </p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>The Escape from Vasto: Complaints of a 15th century Italian Rabbi</strong></em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>February 1st</strong></p>
<p class="p"><em>Avraham Gross, Ben-Gurion University </em></p>
<p class="p"><em></em><em><strong>Liturgy as a Collective and Personal Memorial of 1096</strong></em></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><em><strong></strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><strong>January 24th</strong></p>
<p class="p"><em>Shamma Friedman, Jewish Theological Seminary of America </em></p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Now You See it, Now You Don’t: Can Source- Criticism Perform Magic on Talmudic Passages about Sorcery?</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><em><br /></em></p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Spring Term 2012</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>Wednesday, 30th May</strong></p>
<p class="p">David Sorkin</p>
<p class="p"><strong>Beyond the Secular-Religious Dichotomy: Four
Characteristics of the Religious Enlightenment</strong></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/beyond_dichotomy" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>Monday, 21st May</strong></p>
<p class="p"> Henny Brenner and Michael Brenner<br /></p>
<p class="p"> <strong>From Experience, to Memoir, to History: Henny Brenner in Nazi Dresden</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/from_experience" target="_self">More...</a></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"> <strong>April 23rd</strong></p>
<p class="p">Yohanan Petrovsky-Shtern</p>
<p class="p"><em><strong>Crime and Punishment in the Shtetl (1790-1850)</strong></em></p>
<p class="p"><a href="https://www.ucl.ac.uk/ijs/All_Events/spring_2012/crime_and_punishment">More...</a><br /></p>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong>April</strong><strong> 8th</strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> Amy-Jill Levine<br /> </p>
<p class="p"><strong> </strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><em>Violence
on the Jerusalem-Jericho Road:</em></strong></p>
<p class="p"> <strong><em> Readings and Misreadings of the Parable
of the Good Samaritan</em></strong></p>

<h3 class="heading"></h3>

        <h2 class="heading">Highlights</h2>
<p class="p">The
IJS Autumn programme will be available shortly. Watch this space, and if you
are not on our mailing list please email <a href="mailto:s.benisaac@ucl.ac.uk">s.benisaac@ucl.ac.uk</a>
so that we can keep you fully informed. We look forward to seeing you
after the summer break. </p>

<!-- start main slot where silva content gets rendered--> 
	<h2 class="heading">Summer Term 2011</h2>
<hr class="rule" />
<p class="p"><strong><em><br /></em></strong></p>
<p class="p"><strong><em>June 1st  2011 </em></strong>BOOK LAUNCH AND LECTURE</p>
<p class="p"><br />Ada Rapoport-Albert<br /><br /><em><strong>Women and the Messianic Heresy of Sabbatai Zevi, 1666-1816</strong></em><br /><br /><br />Women are conspicuously absent from the Jewish mystical tradition.  Only the<br />chance survival of scant evidence suggests that, at various times and places, individual Jewish women did pursue the path of mystical piety or prophetic spirituality, but it appears that they were generally highly censured. This contrasts sharply with the fully acknowledged prominence of women in the mystical traditions of both Christianity and Islam.<br /><br />It is against this background that the mystical messianic movement centred on the personality of Sabbatai Zevi (1626-76) stands out as a unique and remarkable exception. Sabbatai Zevi addressed to women a highly original liberationist message, proclaiming that he had come to make them 'as happy as men' by releasing them from the pangs of childbirth and the subjugation to their husbands that were ordained for women as a consequence of the primordial sin. This unprecedented redemptive vision became an integral part of Sabbatian philosophy, which the messianists believed to be unfolding.<br /><br />Their New Law, superseding the Old with the dawning of the messianic era, overturned the traditional Jewish norms that distinguished and regulated relations between the sexes. This was expressed not only in the outlandish ritual transgression of sexual prohibitions, in which Sabbatian women were notoriously implicated, but also in the apparent adoption of the idea  -alien to rabbinic Judaism- that virginity, celibacy, or sexual abstinence were conducive to women's spiritual empowerment.<br /><br />Ada Rapoport-Albert's latest book traces the diverse manifestations of this vision in every phase of Sabbatianism and its offshoots. </p>
<hr class="rule" />

<h3 class="heading"><em>Undzere kinder (Our Children)</em></h3>





<p class="p"><em></em><br /><strong>June 13th  2011</strong><br /><br /><em><strong>Undzere kinder</strong> is a Yiddish film (with English sub-titles) made in 1948<br />The film is one of the only postwar movies made in Yiddish and almost the last full-length Yiddish film to be made. It was also the first film which attempted to deal with the Holocaust. Suppressed by the post-war Polish Communist government as 'pro-Zionist' and lost for over 30 years, Our Children was largely shot on location at an orphanage/school near Lodz. It stars children who were actual survivors of the Holocaust and focuses on how they come to terms with their past.<br /></em><br /></p>
